	```
	    import React, { useEffect, useState } from'react'
	    import Header from'../componets/Header'
	    import'../assets/style/App.scss'
	    import Search from'../componets/Search'
	    import Category from'../componets/Category'
	    import Carousel from'../componets/Carousel'
	    import CarouselItem from'../componets/CarouselItem'
	    import Footer from'../componets/Footer'
	    import useInitialState from'../Hooks/useInitialState'
	    
	    const API = 'http://localhost:3000/initalState'
	    
	    const App = () => {
	        const initialState = useInitialState(API)
	        return (
	            <React.Fragment>
	                <Header />
	                <Search />
	                {initialState.mylist?.length > 0 && 
	                    <Category title="Mi lista">
	                        <Carousel>
	                        {initialState.mylist?.map(item => 
	                            <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item} />
	                        )}
	                        </Carousel>
	                    </Category>
	                }
	                
	                <Category title="Trends de platzi video">
	                    <Carousel>
	                    {initialState.trends?.map(item => 
	                        <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item}/>
	                    )}
	                    </Carousel>
	                </Category>
	                <Category title="Originals de platzi video">
	                    <Carousel>
	                    {initialState.originals?.map(item => 
	                        <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item}/>
	                    )}
	                    </Carousel>
	                </Category>
	                <Footer />
	            </React.Fragment>
	        )}
	    
	    exportdefault App

* **Jos√© Fernando Brice√±o Ru√≠z** (1) [844622](https://platzi.com/comentario/844622/) 

	**useInitialState.js**
	``` 
	    import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
	    
	    const useInitialState = (API) => {
	      const [videos, setVideos] = useState([]);
	      useEffect(() => {
	        fetch(API)
	          .then((response) => response.json())
	          .then((data) => setVideos(data));
	      }, []);
	    
	      return videos;
	    };
	    
	    export default useInitialState;
	    
	```
	
	**App.js**
	``` 
	    import React from"react";
	    import Header from"../components/Header";
	    import Search from"../components/Search";
	    import Categories from"../components/Categories";
	    import Carousel from"../components/Carousel";
	    import CarouselItem from"../components/CarouselItem";
	    import Footer from"../components/Footer";
	    import useInitialState from '../hooks/useInitialState';
	    
	    import "../assets/styles/App.scss";
	    
	    const API = 'http://localhost:3000/initalState';
	    
	    const App = () => {
	      
	      const initialState = useInitialState(API);
	    
	      return initialState.length === 0 ? <h1>Cargando...</h1> : 
	    (
	        <div className="App">
	          <Header />
	          <Search />
	    
	          {initialState.mylist.length > 0 &&
	            <Categories title="Mi lista">
	            <Carousel>
	            {initialState.mylist.map(item =>
	              <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item} />
	              )}
	            </Carousel>
	            </Categories>
	          }
	    
	          <Categories title="Tendencias">
	            <Carousel>
	            {initialState.trends.map(item =>
	              <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item} />
	              )}
	            </Carousel>
	          </Categories>
	    
	          <Categories title="Originales de Platzi Video">
	          <Carousel>
	          {initialState.originals.map(item =>
	            <CarouselItem key={item.id} {...item} />
	            )}
	          </Carousel>
	          </Categories>
	          <Footer />
	        </div>
	      );
	    };
	    
	    export default App;
	    
	```

* **JESUS ALMIRCAR CASTELLANOS** (1) [786458](https://platzi.com/comentario/786458/) 

	```
	    import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
	    
	    const useInitialState = (API) => {
	      const [videos, setVideos] = useState({ mylist: [], trends: [], originals: [] });
	      useEffect(() => {
	        fetch(API)
	          .then((response) => response.json())
	          .then((data) => setVideos(data));
	      }, []);
	      return videos;
	    };
	    export default useInitialState;

## 0270. PropTypes [21950](https://platzi.com/clases/1651-react-ejs/21950-proptypes/)

### Descripci√≥n:


Los **PropTypes** son una propiedad de nuestros componentes que nos permiten especificar qu√© tipo de elementos son nuestras props: arrays, strings, n√∫meros, etc.

Instalaci√≥n de PropTypes:
``` 
    npm install --save prop-types
    
```

Uso de PropTypes:
``` 
    import React from 'react';
    import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
    
    const Component = ({ name, lastName, age, list }) => {
      // ...
    };
    
    Component.propTypes = {
      name: PropTypes.string,
      lastName: PropTypes.string,
      age: PropTypes.number,
      list: PropTypes.array,
    };
    
    export default Component;
    
```

Por defecto, enviar todas nuestras props es opcional, pero con los `propTypes` podemos especificar cu√°les props son obligatorias para que nuestro componente funcione correctamente con el atributo `isRequired`.
``` 
    Component.propTypes = {
      name: PropTypes.string.isRequired, // obligatorio
      lastName: PropTypes.string.isRequired, // obligatorio
      age: PropTypes.number, // opcional,
      list: PropTypes.array, // opcional
    };
    
```

### Links:

* [Verificaci√≥n de tipos con PropTypes ‚Äì React](https://es.reactjs.org/docs/typechecking-with-proptypes.html)

		Carlos Sampol nos ense√±o en un meetup de Platzi que usar el spread operator para enviar tus props es como enviar una cajita sin saber qu√© es lo que hay por dentro.
		
		El objetivo de esta regla es que no uses el _spread operator_ para que tengas que pasar una _prop_ a la vez y tengas control total sobre la informaci√≥n que env√≠as a tus componentes.
		
		Si no quieres que te marquen esos errores solo debes deshabilitar esa regla en ESLint. üòâ
		
		<https://github.com/yannickcr/eslint-plugin-react/blob/master/docs/rules/jsx-props-no-spreading.md>

## 0280. Debuggeando React con React DevTools [21951](https://platzi.com/clases/1651-react-ejs/21951-debuggeando-react-con-react-devtools/)

### Descripci√≥n:


**React DevTools** es una herramienta muy parecida al Inspector de Elementos. Nos permite visualizar, analizar e interactuar con nuestros componentes de React desde el navegador.

Encuentra m√°s informaci√≥n sobre est√° herramienta en: [github.com/facebook/react-devtools](https://github.com/facebook/react-devtools).

### Links:

* [GitHub - facebook/react-devtools: An extension that allows inspection of React component hierarchy in the Chrome and Firefox Developer Tools.](https://github.com/facebook/react-devtools)

* [React Developer Tools - Chrome Web Store](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/react-developer-tools/fmkadmapgofadopljbjfkapdkoienihi)

* [React Developer Tools ‚Äì Get this Extension for ü¶ä Firefox (en-US)](https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/firefox/addon/react-devtools/)

* [Page not found ¬∑ GitHub ¬∑ GitHub](https://github.com/facebook/react-devtools/blob/master/packages/react-devtools/README.md)

* [react-devtools  -  npm](https://www.npmjs.com/package/react-devtools)
